/kind feature

#### What this PR does / why we need it:

* Introduce new ComposableJob interface for jobs which has to be composed of different API objects.

* Add ComposableJob implementation for pod groups.

* Add webhook checks for pod group labels and annotations.

#### Which issue(s) this PR fixes:
<!--
*Automatically closes linked issue when PR is merged.
Usage: `Fixes #<issue number>`, or `Fixes (paste link of issue)`.
_If PR is about `failing-tests or flakes`, please post the related issues/tests in a comment and do not use `Fixes`_*
-->
Related issue: #976

#### Does this PR introduce a user-facing change?

If yes, a release note is required:
Enter your extended release note in the block below. If the PR requires additional action from users switching to the new release, include the string "action required".
-->
```release-note
Add support for groups of plain Pods.
```

- **pkg/controller/jobframework/reconciler.go:654** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-11-14T20:23:59Z
```diff
@@ -583,6 +612,26 @@ func (r *JobReconciler) removeFinalizer(ctx context.Context, wl *kueue.Workload)
 func (r *JobReconciler) constructWorkload(ctx context.Context, job GenericJob, object client.Object) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
 	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
 
+	if cj, implements := job.(ComposableJob); implements {
+		wl, err := cj.ConstructWorkload(ctx, r.client, r.record)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		wl.Spec.PodSets = ResetMinCounts(wl.Spec.PodSets)
+
+		priorityClassName, source, p, err := r.extractPriority(ctx, wl.Spec.PodSets, job)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		wl.Spec.PriorityClassName = priorityClassName
+		wl.Spec.Priority = &p
+		wl.Spec.PriorityClassSource = source
+
+		return wl, nil
```

  This is common code.
  
  Maybe `constructWorkload` should focus on getting the basics of the workload, and there could be another function `prepareWorkload` that adds the priority bits.

- **pkg/controller/jobs/pod/pod_controller.go:569** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-11-14T20:35:26Z
```diff
@@ -229,6 +264,276 @@ func (p *Pod) Skip() bool {
 	return false
 }
 
+func (p *Pod) GetGroupName() string {
+	return p.Object().GetLabels()[GroupNameLabel]
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) GetGroupTotalCount() (int, error) {
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("pod doesn't have a '%s' label", GroupNameLabel)
+	}
+
+	gtcAnnotation, ok := p.Object().GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation]
+	if !ok {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	gtc, err := strconv.Atoi(gtcAnnotation)
+	if err != nil {
+		return 0, err
+	}
+
+	if gtc < 1 {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("incorrect annotation value '%s=%s': group total count should be greater than zero",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation, gtcAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	return gtc, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup corev1.PodList) ([]kueue.PodSet, error) {
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.GetGroupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+
+	var (
+		resultPodSets []kueue.PodSet
+	)
+
+	for _, podInGroup := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		tc, err := strconv.Atoi(podInGroup.GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation])
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation from the pod '%s': %w",
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				podInGroup.GetName(),
+				err)
+		}
+		if tc != groupTotalCount {
+			// ToDo: Add a warning event
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("pods '%s' and '%s' has different '%s' values: %d!=%d",
+				p.GetName(), podInGroup.GetName(),
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				groupTotalCount, tc)
+		}
+
+		roleHash, ok := podInGroup.Annotations[RoleHashAnnotation]
+		if !ok {
+			roleHash, err = getRoleHash(fromObject(&podInGroup))
+		}
+
+		roleHash = roleHash[:8]
+
+		podRoleFound := false
+		for psi := range resultPodSets {
+			if resultPodSets[psi].Name == roleHash {
+				podRoleFound = true
+				resultPodSets[psi].Count++
+			}
+		}
+
+		if !podRoleFound {
+			podSet := fromObject(&podInGroup).PodSets()
+			podSet[0].Name = roleHash
+
+			resultPodSets = append(resultPodSets, podSet[0])
+		}
+	}
+
+	return resultPodSets, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) ConstructWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets     []kueue.PodSet
+		podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	)
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: p.GetGroupName(),
+		}); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.GetGroupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podsInGroup.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+		}
+
+		podSets, err = p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	wl := &kueue.Workload{
+		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+			Namespace:  p.GetNamespace(),
+			Labels:     map[string]string{},
+			Finalizers: []string{kueue.ResourceInUseFinalizerName},
+		},
+		Spec: kueue.WorkloadSpec{
+			PodSets:   podSets,
+			QueueName: jobframework.QueueName(p),
+		},
+	}
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		wl.Name = jobframework.GetWorkloadNameForOwnerWithGVK(p.GetName(), p.GVK())
+	} else {
+		wl.Name = p.GetGroupName()
+	}
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		jobUid := string(p.Object().GetUID())
+		if errs := validation.IsValidLabelValue(jobUid); len(errs) == 0 {
+			wl.Labels[controllerconsts.JobUIDLabel] = jobUid
+		} else {
+			log.V(2).Info(
+				"Validation of the owner job UID label has failed. Creating workload without the label.",
+				"ValidationErrors", errs,
+				"LabelValue", jobUid,
+			)
+		}
+
+		// add the owner ref
+		if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(p.Object(), wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		if err := controllerutil.SetOwnerReference(&pod, wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	return wl, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx context.Context, c client.Client) (*kueue.Workload, []*kueue.Workload, *kueue.WorkloadList, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+	groupName := p.GetGroupName()
+
+	if groupName == "" {
+		return jobframework.FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx, c, p, object)
+	}
+
+	// Find a matching workload first if there is one.
+	var toDelete []*kueue.Workload
+	var match *kueue.Workload
+	workloads := &kueue.WorkloadList{}
+
+	if err := c.List(ctx, workloads, client.InNamespace(object.GetNamespace()),
+		client.MatchingFields{WorkloadNameKey: p.GetGroupName()}); err != nil {
+		log.Error(err, "Unable to list related workloads")
+		return nil, nil, nil, err
+	}
```

  this should be `c.Get` instead

```diff
+
+	return resultPodSets, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) ConstructWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets     []kueue.PodSet
+		podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	)
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: p.GetGroupName(),
+		}); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.GetGroupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podsInGroup.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+		}
+
+		podSets, err = p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	wl := &kueue.Workload{
+		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+			Namespace:  p.GetNamespace(),
+			Labels:     map[string]string{},
+			Finalizers: []string{kueue.ResourceInUseFinalizerName},
+		},
+		Spec: kueue.WorkloadSpec{
+			PodSets:   podSets,
+			QueueName: jobframework.QueueName(p),
+		},
+	}
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		wl.Name = jobframework.GetWorkloadNameForOwnerWithGVK(p.GetName(), p.GVK())
+	} else {
+		wl.Name = p.GetGroupName()
+	}
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		jobUid := string(p.Object().GetUID())
+		if errs := validation.IsValidLabelValue(jobUid); len(errs) == 0 {
+			wl.Labels[controllerconsts.JobUIDLabel] = jobUid
+		} else {
+			log.V(2).Info(
+				"Validation of the owner job UID label has failed. Creating workload without the label.",
+				"ValidationErrors", errs,
+				"LabelValue", jobUid,
+			)
+		}
+
+		// add the owner ref
+		if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(p.Object(), wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		if err := controllerutil.SetOwnerReference(&pod, wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	return wl, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx context.Context, c client.Client) (*kueue.Workload, []*kueue.Workload, *kueue.WorkloadList, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+	groupName := p.GetGroupName()
+
+	if groupName == "" {
+		return jobframework.FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx, c, p, object)
+	}
+
+	// Find a matching workload first if there is one.
+	var toDelete []*kueue.Workload
+	var match *kueue.Workload
+	workloads := &kueue.WorkloadList{}
+
+	if err := c.List(ctx, workloads, client.InNamespace(object.GetNamespace()),
+		client.MatchingFields{WorkloadNameKey: p.GetGroupName()}); err != nil {
+		log.Error(err, "Unable to list related workloads")
+		return nil, nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	var podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+		GroupNameLabel: p.GetGroupName(),
+	}); err != nil {
+		return nil, nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	jobPodSets, err := p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	for i := range workloads.Items {
+		w := &workloads.Items[i]
+		if match == nil && p.equivalentToWorkload(w, jobPodSets) {
+			match = w
+		} else {
+			toDelete = append(toDelete, w)
+		}
+	}
+
+	return match, toDelete, workloads, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) equivalentToWorkload(wl *kueue.Workload, jobPodSets []kueue.PodSet) bool {
+	if wl.GetName() != p.GetGroupName() {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	if len(jobPodSets) != len(wl.Spec.PodSets) {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	for i := range wl.Spec.PodSets {
+		if wl.Spec.PodSets[i].Count != jobPodSets[i].Count {
+			return false
+		}
+		if wl.Spec.PodSets[i].Name != jobPodSets[i].Name {
+			return false
+		}
+	}
+
+	return true
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) IsComposableJobFinished(ctx context.Context, c client.Client) (metav1.Condition, bool) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	groupName := p.GetGroupName()
+	if groupName == "" {
+		return p.Finished()
+	}
+
+	var podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+		GroupNameLabel: groupName,
+	}); err != nil {
+		return metav1.Condition{}, false
+	}
+
+	failedPodCount := 0
+
+	for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		if pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodFailed {
+			failedPodCount++
+		}
+
+		podJob := fromObject(&pod)
+		if _, finished := podJob.Finished(); !finished {
+			return metav1.Condition{}, false
+		}
+	}
+
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.GetGroupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		log.V(2).Error(err, "Error while checking if pod group is finished", "Pod.Name", p.Name)
+		return metav1.Condition{}, false
+	}
+
+	condition := metav1.Condition{
+		Type:   kueue.WorkloadFinished,
+		Status: metav1.ConditionTrue,
```

  are we always returning true?
  The job should only considered finished if the number of successful pods equals the number of pods for the group.

```diff
+		if !ok {
+			return nil
+		}
+		return []string{wl.ObjectMeta.Name}
+	}); err != nil {
+		return err
+	}
```

- **pkg/controller/jobs/pod/pod_controller.go:415** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-11-14T21:14:56Z
```diff
@@ -229,6 +264,276 @@ func (p *Pod) Skip() bool {
 	return false
 }
 
+func (p *Pod) GetGroupName() string {
+	return p.Object().GetLabels()[GroupNameLabel]
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) GetGroupTotalCount() (int, error) {
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("pod doesn't have a '%s' label", GroupNameLabel)
+	}
+
+	gtcAnnotation, ok := p.Object().GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation]
+	if !ok {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	gtc, err := strconv.Atoi(gtcAnnotation)
+	if err != nil {
+		return 0, err
+	}
+
+	if gtc < 1 {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("incorrect annotation value '%s=%s': group total count should be greater than zero",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation, gtcAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	return gtc, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup corev1.PodList) ([]kueue.PodSet, error) {
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.GetGroupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+
+	var (
+		resultPodSets []kueue.PodSet
+	)
+
+	for _, podInGroup := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		tc, err := strconv.Atoi(podInGroup.GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation])
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation from the pod '%s': %w",
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				podInGroup.GetName(),
+				err)
+		}
+		if tc != groupTotalCount {
+			// ToDo: Add a warning event
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("pods '%s' and '%s' has different '%s' values: %d!=%d",
+				p.GetName(), podInGroup.GetName(),
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				groupTotalCount, tc)
+		}
+
+		roleHash, ok := podInGroup.Annotations[RoleHashAnnotation]
+		if !ok {
+			roleHash, err = getRoleHash(fromObject(&podInGroup))
+		}
+
+		roleHash = roleHash[:8]
+
+		podRoleFound := false
+		for psi := range resultPodSets {
+			if resultPodSets[psi].Name == roleHash {
+				podRoleFound = true
+				resultPodSets[psi].Count++
+			}
+		}
+
+		if !podRoleFound {
+			podSet := fromObject(&podInGroup).PodSets()
+			podSet[0].Name = roleHash
+
+			resultPodSets = append(resultPodSets, podSet[0])
+		}
+	}
+
+	return resultPodSets, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) ConstructWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets     []kueue.PodSet
+		podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	)
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: p.GetGroupName(),
+		}); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.GetGroupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podsInGroup.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+		}
+
+		podSets, err = p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	wl := &kueue.Workload{
+		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+			Namespace:  p.GetNamespace(),
+			Labels:     map[string]string{},
+			Finalizers: []string{kueue.ResourceInUseFinalizerName},
+		},
+		Spec: kueue.WorkloadSpec{
+			PodSets:   podSets,
+			QueueName: jobframework.QueueName(p),
+		},
+	}
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		wl.Name = jobframework.GetWorkloadNameForOwnerWithGVK(p.GetName(), p.GVK())
+	} else {
+		wl.Name = p.GetGroupName()
+	}
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		jobUid := string(p.Object().GetUID())
+		if errs := validation.IsValidLabelValue(jobUid); len(errs) == 0 {
+			wl.Labels[controllerconsts.JobUIDLabel] = jobUid
+		} else {
+			log.V(2).Info(
+				"Validation of the owner job UID label has failed. Creating workload without the label.",
+				"ValidationErrors", errs,
+				"LabelValue", jobUid,
+			)
+		}
+
+		// add the owner ref
+		if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(p.Object(), wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
```

  else?

```diff
+func FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, job GenericJob, object client.Object) (match *kueue.Workload, toDelete []*kueue.Workload, workloads *kueue.WorkloadList, err error) {
```

```diff
+	gtcAnnotation, ok := p.Object().GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation]
+	if !ok {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	gtc, err := strconv.Atoi(gtcAnnotation)
+	if err != nil {
+		return 0, err
+	}
+
+	if gtc < 1 {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("incorrect annotation value '%s=%s': group total count should be greater than zero",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation, gtcAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	return gtc, nil
+}

+func (p *Pod) constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup corev1.PodList) ([]kueue.PodSet, error) {
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}

+	var (
+		resultPodSets []kueue.PodSet
+	)
```

  ```suggestion
  	var resultPodSets []kueue.PodSet
  ```

- **pkg/controller/jobs/pod/pod_controller.go:363** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-11-15T16:18:21Z
```diff
@@ -229,6 +255,266 @@ func (p *Pod) Skip() bool {
 	return false
 }
 
+func (p *Pod) groupName() string {
+	return p.Object().GetLabels()[GroupNameLabel]
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) groupTotalCount() (int, error) {
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("pod doesn't have a '%s' label", GroupNameLabel)
+	}
+
+	gtcAnnotation, ok := p.Object().GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation]
+	if !ok {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	gtc, err := strconv.Atoi(gtcAnnotation)
+	if err != nil {
+		return 0, err
+	}
+
+	if gtc < 1 {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("incorrect annotation value '%s=%s': group total count should be greater than zero",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation, gtcAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	return gtc, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup corev1.PodList) ([]kueue.PodSet, error) {
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+
+	var (
+		resultPodSets []kueue.PodSet
+	)
+
+	for _, podInGroup := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		tc, err := strconv.Atoi(podInGroup.GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation])
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation from the pod '%s': %w",
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				podInGroup.GetName(),
+				err)
+		}
+		if tc != groupTotalCount {
+			// ToDo: Add a warning event
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("pods '%s' and '%s' has different '%s' values: %d!=%d",
+				p.GetName(), podInGroup.GetName(),
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				groupTotalCount, tc)
+		}
+
+		roleHash, ok := podInGroup.Annotations[RoleHashAnnotation]
+		if !ok {
+			roleHash, err = getRoleHash(fromObject(&podInGroup))
+		}
+
+		roleHash = roleHash[:8]
+
+		podRoleFound := false
+		for psi := range resultPodSets {
+			if resultPodSets[psi].Name == roleHash {
+				podRoleFound = true
+				resultPodSets[psi].Count++
+			}
+		}
+
+		if !podRoleFound {
+			podSet := fromObject(&podInGroup).PodSets()
+			podSet[0].Name = roleHash
+
+			resultPodSets = append(resultPodSets, podSet[0])
+		}
+	}
+
+	return resultPodSets, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) ConstructComposableWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets     []kueue.PodSet
+		podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	)
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: p.groupName(),
+		}); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podsInGroup.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
```

  if you return an error, the Pod sync will be retried immediately. We don't want that, we would only want to retry once a new pod is observed.
  
  To do this, we might need to create an `UnretriableError` struct that we can ignore from the generic reconciler. Somewhat similar to how we ignore `NotFound` errors.

```diff
+		resultPodSets []kueue.PodSet

+		tc, err := strconv.Atoi(podInGroup.GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation])

+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation from the pod '%s': %w",
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				podInGroup.GetName(),
+				err)
+		}
+		if tc != groupTotalCount {
+			// ToDo: Add a warning event
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("pods '%s' and '%s' has different '%s' values: %d!=%d",
+				p.GetName(), podInGroup.GetName(),
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				groupTotalCount, tc)

+			}

+func (p *Pod) ConstructComposableWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets     []kueue.PodSet
+		podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	)
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: p.groupName(),
+		}); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podsInGroup.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+		}
+
+		podSets, err = p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	wl := &kueue.Workload{
+		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+			Namespace:  p.GetNamespace(),
+			Labels:     map[string]string{},
+			Finalizers: []string{kueue.ResourceInUseFinalizerName},
+		},
+		Spec: kueue.WorkloadSpec{
+			PodSets:   podSets,
+			QueueName: jobframework.QueueName(p),
+		},
+	}
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		wl.Name = jobframework.GetWorkloadNameForOwnerWithGVK(p.GetName(), p.GVK())
+		jobUid := string(p.Object().GetUID())
+		if errs := validation.IsValidLabelValue(jobUid); len(errs) == 0 {
+			wl.Labels[controllerconsts.JobUIDLabel] = jobUid
+		} else {
+			log.V(2).Info(
+				"Validation of the owner job UID label has failed. Creating workload without the label.",
+				"ValidationErrors", errs,
+				"LabelValue", jobUid,
+			)
+		}
+
+		// add the owner ref
+		if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(p.Object(), wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	} else {
+		wl.Name = p.groupName()
+		for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+			if err := controllerutil.SetOwnerReference(&pod, wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
```

```diff
+func (p *Pod) ConstructComposableWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets     []kueue.PodSet
+		podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	)
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: p.groupName(),
+		}); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podsInGroup.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+		}
+
+		podSets, err = p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	wl := &kueue.Workload{
+		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+			Namespace:  p.GetNamespace(),
+			Labels:     map[string]string{},
+			Finalizers: []string{kueue.ResourceInUseFinalizerName},
+		},
+		Spec: kueue.WorkloadSpec{
+			PodSets:   podSets,
+			QueueName: jobframework.QueueName(p),
+		},
+	}
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		wl.Name = jobframework.GetWorkloadNameForOwnerWithGVK(p.GetName(), p.GVK())
+		jobUid := string(p.Object().GetUID())
+		if errs := validation.IsValidLabelValue(jobUid); len(errs) == 0 {
+			wl.Labels[controllerconsts.JobUIDLabel] = jobUid
+		} else {
+			log.V(2).Info(
+				"Validation of the owner job UID label has failed. Creating workload without the label.",
+				"ValidationErrors", errs,
+				"LabelValue", jobUid,
+			)
+		}
+
+		// add the owner ref
+		if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(p.Object(), wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	} else {
+		wl.Name = p.groupName()
+		for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+			if err := controllerutil.SetOwnerReference(&pod, wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+				return nil, err
+			}
+		}
+	}
+
+	return wl, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx context.Context, c client.Client) (*kueue.Workload, []*kueue.Workload, *kueue.WorkloadList, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+	groupName := p.groupName()
+
+	if groupName == "" {
+		return jobframework.FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx, c, p, object)
+	}
+
+	// Find a matching workload first if there is one.
+	workload := &kueue.Workload{}

+		if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+			return nil, nil, nil, nil
+		}
+		log.Error(err, "Unable to list related workloads")
```

  ```suggestion
  		log.Error(err, "Unable to get related workloads")
  ```

- **pkg/controller/jobs/pod/pod_controller.go:527** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-11-15T16:36:55Z
```diff
@@ -229,6 +264,276 @@ func (p *Pod) Skip() bool {
 	return false
 }
 
+func (p *Pod) GetGroupName() string {
+	return p.Object().GetLabels()[GroupNameLabel]
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) GetGroupTotalCount() (int, error) {
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("pod doesn't have a '%s' label", GroupNameLabel)
+	}
+
+	gtcAnnotation, ok := p.Object().GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation]
+	if !ok {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	gtc, err := strconv.Atoi(gtcAnnotation)
+	if err != nil {
+		return 0, err
+	}
+
+	if gtc < 1 {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("incorrect annotation value '%s=%s': group total count should be greater than zero",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation, gtcAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	return gtc, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup corev1.PodList) ([]kueue.PodSet, error) {
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.GetGroupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+
+	var (
+		resultPodSets []kueue.PodSet
+	)
+
+	for _, podInGroup := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		tc, err := strconv.Atoi(podInGroup.GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation])
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation from the pod '%s': %w",
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				podInGroup.GetName(),
+				err)
+		}
+		if tc != groupTotalCount {
+			// ToDo: Add a warning event
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("pods '%s' and '%s' has different '%s' values: %d!=%d",
+				p.GetName(), podInGroup.GetName(),
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				groupTotalCount, tc)
+		}
+
+		roleHash, ok := podInGroup.Annotations[RoleHashAnnotation]
+		if !ok {
+			roleHash, err = getRoleHash(fromObject(&podInGroup))
+		}
+
+		roleHash = roleHash[:8]
+
+		podRoleFound := false
+		for psi := range resultPodSets {
+			if resultPodSets[psi].Name == roleHash {
+				podRoleFound = true
+				resultPodSets[psi].Count++
+			}
+		}
+
+		if !podRoleFound {
+			podSet := fromObject(&podInGroup).PodSets()
+			podSet[0].Name = roleHash
+
+			resultPodSets = append(resultPodSets, podSet[0])
+		}
+	}
+
+	return resultPodSets, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) ConstructWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets     []kueue.PodSet
+		podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	)
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: p.GetGroupName(),
+		}); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.GetGroupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podsInGroup.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+		}
+
+		podSets, err = p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	wl := &kueue.Workload{
+		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+			Namespace:  p.GetNamespace(),
+			Labels:     map[string]string{},
+			Finalizers: []string{kueue.ResourceInUseFinalizerName},
+		},
+		Spec: kueue.WorkloadSpec{
+			PodSets:   podSets,
+			QueueName: jobframework.QueueName(p),
+		},
+	}
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		wl.Name = jobframework.GetWorkloadNameForOwnerWithGVK(p.GetName(), p.GVK())
+	} else {
+		wl.Name = p.GetGroupName()
+	}
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		jobUid := string(p.Object().GetUID())
+		if errs := validation.IsValidLabelValue(jobUid); len(errs) == 0 {
+			wl.Labels[controllerconsts.JobUIDLabel] = jobUid
+		} else {
+			log.V(2).Info(
+				"Validation of the owner job UID label has failed. Creating workload without the label.",
+				"ValidationErrors", errs,
+				"LabelValue", jobUid,
+			)
+		}
+
+		// add the owner ref
+		if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(p.Object(), wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		if err := controllerutil.SetOwnerReference(&pod, wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	return wl, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx context.Context, c client.Client) (*kueue.Workload, []*kueue.Workload, *kueue.WorkloadList, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+	groupName := p.GetGroupName()
+
+	if groupName == "" {
+		return jobframework.FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx, c, p, object)
+	}
+
+	// Find a matching workload first if there is one.
+	var toDelete []*kueue.Workload
+	var match *kueue.Workload
+	workloads := &kueue.WorkloadList{}
+
+	if err := c.List(ctx, workloads, client.InNamespace(object.GetNamespace()),
+		client.MatchingFields{WorkloadNameKey: p.GetGroupName()}); err != nil {
+		log.Error(err, "Unable to list related workloads")
+		return nil, nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	var podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+		GroupNameLabel: p.GetGroupName(),
+	}); err != nil {
+		return nil, nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	jobPodSets, err := p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	for i := range workloads.Items {
+		w := &workloads.Items[i]
+		if match == nil && p.equivalentToWorkload(w, jobPodSets) {
+			match = w
+		} else {
+			toDelete = append(toDelete, w)
+		}
+	}
+
+	return match, toDelete, workloads, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) equivalentToWorkload(wl *kueue.Workload, jobPodSets []kueue.PodSet) bool {
+	if wl.GetName() != p.GetGroupName() {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	if len(jobPodSets) != len(wl.Spec.PodSets) {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	for i := range wl.Spec.PodSets {
+		if wl.Spec.PodSets[i].Count != jobPodSets[i].Count {
+			return false
+		}
+		if wl.Spec.PodSets[i].Name != jobPodSets[i].Name {
+			return false
+		}
+	}
+
+	return true
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) IsComposableJobFinished(ctx context.Context, c client.Client) (metav1.Condition, bool) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	groupName := p.GetGroupName()
+	if groupName == "" {
+		return p.Finished()
+	}
+
+	var podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+		GroupNameLabel: groupName,
+	}); err != nil {
+		return metav1.Condition{}, false
+	}
+
+	failedPodCount := 0
+
+	for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		if pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodFailed {
+			failedPodCount++
+		}
+
+		podJob := fromObject(&pod)
+		if _, finished := podJob.Finished(); !finished {
+			return metav1.Condition{}, false
+		}
+	}
+
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.GetGroupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		log.V(2).Error(err, "Error while checking if pod group is finished", "Pod.Name", p.Name)
+		return metav1.Condition{}, false
+	}
+
+	condition := metav1.Condition{
+		Type:   kueue.WorkloadFinished,
+		Status: metav1.ConditionTrue,
```

  Still pending resolution.

- **pkg/controller/jobs/pod/pod_webhook.go:141** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-11-15T16:51:46Z
```diff
@@ -77,6 +86,77 @@ func SetupWebhook(mgr ctrl.Manager, opts ...jobframework.Option) error {
 
 var _ webhook.CustomDefaulter = &PodWebhook{}
 
+func omitKueueLabels(l map[string]string) map[string]string {
+	result := map[string]string{}
+
+	for key, value := range l {
+		if !strings.HasPrefix(key, "kueue.x-k8s.io/") {
+			result[key] = value
+		}
+	}
+	return result
+}
+
+func containersShape(containers []corev1.Container) (result []map[string]interface{}) {
+	for _, c := range containers {
+		result = append(result, map[string]interface{}{
+			"image": c.Image,
+			"resources": map[string]interface{}{
+				"requests": c.Resources.Requests,
+			},
+			"ports": c.Ports,
+		})
+	}
+
+	return result
+}
+
+func getRoleHash(p *Pod) (string, error) {
+
+	shape := map[string]interface{}{
+		"metadata": map[string]interface{}{
+			"labels": omitKueueLabels(p.ObjectMeta.Labels),
+		},
+		"spec": map[string]interface{}{
+			"initContainers":            containersShape(p.Spec.InitContainers),
+			"containers":                containersShape(p.Spec.Containers),
+			"nodeSelector":              p.Spec.NodeSelector,
+			"affinity":                  p.Spec.Affinity,
+			"tolerations":               p.Spec.Tolerations,
+			"runtimeClassName":          p.Spec.RuntimeClassName,
+			"priority":                  p.Spec.Priority,
+			"preemptionPolicy":          p.Spec.PreemptionPolicy,
+			"topologySpreadConstraints": p.Spec.TopologySpreadConstraints,
+			"overhead":                  p.Spec.Overhead,
+			"volumes":                   p.Spec.Volumes,
+			"resourceClaims":            p.Spec.ResourceClaims,
+		},
+	}
+
+	shapeJson, err := json.Marshal(shape)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	return fmt.Sprintf("%x", sha256.Sum256(shapeJson)), nil
```

  I think I saw in other places that you were only taking 8 characters? Let's try to do it in one place, and this function seems like the best place.

```diff
@@ -229,6 +255,266 @@ func (p *Pod) Skip() bool {
 	return false
 }
 
+func (p *Pod) groupName() string {
+	return p.Object().GetLabels()[GroupNameLabel]
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) groupTotalCount() (int, error) {
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("pod doesn't have a '%s' label", GroupNameLabel)
+	}
+
+	gtcAnnotation, ok := p.Object().GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation]
+	if !ok {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	gtc, err := strconv.Atoi(gtcAnnotation)
+	if err != nil {
+		return 0, err
+	}
+
+	if gtc < 1 {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("incorrect annotation value '%s=%s': group total count should be greater than zero",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation, gtcAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	return gtc, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup corev1.PodList) ([]kueue.PodSet, error) {
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+
+	var (
+		resultPodSets []kueue.PodSet
+	)
+
+	for _, podInGroup := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		tc, err := strconv.Atoi(podInGroup.GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation])
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation from the pod '%s': %w",
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				podInGroup.GetName(),
+				err)
+		}
+		if tc != groupTotalCount {
+			// ToDo: Add a warning event
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("pods '%s' and '%s' has different '%s' values: %d!=%d",
+				p.GetName(), podInGroup.GetName(),
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				groupTotalCount, tc)
+		}
+
+		roleHash, ok := podInGroup.Annotations[RoleHashAnnotation]
+		if !ok {
+			roleHash, err = getRoleHash(fromObject(&podInGroup))
+		}
+
+		roleHash = roleHash[:8]
+
+		podRoleFound := false
+		for psi := range resultPodSets {
+			if resultPodSets[psi].Name == roleHash {
+				podRoleFound = true
+				resultPodSets[psi].Count++
+			}
+		}
+
+		if !podRoleFound {
+			podSet := fromObject(&podInGroup).PodSets()
+			podSet[0].Name = roleHash
+
+			resultPodSets = append(resultPodSets, podSet[0])
+		}
+	}
+
+	return resultPodSets, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) ConstructComposableWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets     []kueue.PodSet
+		podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	)
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: p.groupName(),
+		}); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podsInGroup.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
```

  JFYI we could use the [`TerminalError`](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/controller-runtime/blob/06fb2e9592987c3182bae373f83e4b7e6f0b9e2b/pkg/reconcile/reconcile.go#L113) from `controller-runtime` here, but I will implement a custom error, since we don't need those types of errors coming up in metrics.

```diff
+func (p *Pod) GetGroupName() string {
+	return p.Object().GetLabels()[GroupNameLabel]

+
+func (p *Pod) GetGroupTotalCount() (int, error) {

+			if resultPodSets[psi].Name == roleHash {
+				podRoleFound = true
+				resultPodSets[psi].Count++
+			}

+func (p *Pod) ConstructWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets     []kueue.PodSet
+		podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	)
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: p.GetGroupName(),
+		}); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.GetGroupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podsInGroup.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+		}
+
+		podSets, err = p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	wl := &kueue.Workload{
+		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+			Namespace:  p.GetNamespace(),
+			Labels:     map[string]string{},
+			Finalizers: []string{kueue.ResourceInUseFinalizerName},
+		},
+		Spec: kueue.WorkloadSpec{
+			PodSets:   podSets,
+			QueueName: jobframework.QueueName(p),
+		},
+	}
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		wl.Name = jobframework.GetWorkloadNameForOwnerWithGVK(p.GetName(), p.GVK())
+	} else {
+		wl.Name = p.GetGroupName()
+	}
+
+	if p.GetGroupName() == "" {
+		jobUid := string(p.Object().GetUID())
+		if errs := validation.IsValidLabelValue(jobUid); len(errs) == 0 {
+			wl.Labels[controllerconsts.JobUIDLabel] = jobUid
+		} else {
+			log.V(2).Info(
+				"Validation of the owner job UID label has failed. Creating workload without the label.",
+				"ValidationErrors", errs,
+				"LabelValue", jobUid,
+			)
+		}
+
+		// add the owner ref
+		if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(p.Object(), wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		if err := controllerutil.SetOwnerReference(&pod, wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	return wl, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx context.Context, c client.Client) (*kueue.Workload, []*kueue.Workload, *kueue.WorkloadList, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+	groupName := p.GetGroupName()
+
+	if groupName == "" {
+		return jobframework.FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx, c, p, object)
+	}
+
+	// Find a matching workload first if there is one.
+	var toDelete []*kueue.Workload
+	var match *kueue.Workload
+	workloads := &kueue.WorkloadList{}
+
+	if err := c.List(ctx, workloads, client.InNamespace(object.GetNamespace()),
+		client.MatchingFields{WorkloadNameKey: p.GetGroupName()}); err != nil {
+		log.Error(err, "Unable to list related workloads")
+		return nil, nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	var podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+		GroupNameLabel: p.GetGroupName(),
+	}); err != nil {
+		return nil, nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	jobPodSets, err := p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	for i := range workloads.Items {
+		w := &workloads.Items[i]
+		if match == nil && p.equivalentToWorkload(w, jobPodSets) {
+			match = w
+		} else {
+			toDelete = append(toDelete, w)
+		}
+	}
+
+	return match, toDelete, workloads, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) equivalentToWorkload(wl *kueue.Workload, jobPodSets []kueue.PodSet) bool {
+	if wl.GetName() != p.GetGroupName() {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	if len(jobPodSets) != len(wl.Spec.PodSets) {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	for i := range wl.Spec.PodSets {
+		if wl.Spec.PodSets[i].Count != jobPodSets[i].Count {
+			return false
+		}
+		if wl.Spec.PodSets[i].Name != jobPodSets[i].Name {
+			return false
+		}
+	}
+
+	return true
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) IsComposableJobFinished(ctx context.Context, c client.Client) (metav1.Condition, bool) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	groupName := p.GetGroupName()
+	if groupName == "" {
+		return p.Finished()
+	}
+
+	var podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+		GroupNameLabel: groupName,
+	}); err != nil {
+		return metav1.Condition{}, false
+	}
+
+	failedPodCount := 0
+
+	for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		if pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodFailed {
+			failedPodCount++
+		}
+
+		podJob := fromObject(&pod)
+		if _, finished := podJob.Finished(); !finished {
+			return metav1.Condition{}, false
+		}
+	}
+
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.GetGroupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		log.V(2).Error(err, "Error while checking if pod group is finished", "Pod.Name", p.Name)
+		return metav1.Condition{}, false
+	}
+
+	condition := metav1.Condition{
+		Type:   kueue.WorkloadFinished,
+		Status: metav1.ConditionTrue,
```

  Changed in https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/1319/commits/fb5a4eb591521e5e3e2d7acfb4b6268a697b52e9

```diff
 func (r *JobReconciler) constructWorkload(ctx context.Context, job GenericJob, object client.Object) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
 	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
 
+	if cj, implements := job.(ComposableJob); implements {
+		wl, err := cj.ConstructWorkload(ctx, r.client, r.record)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		wl.Spec.PodSets = ResetMinCounts(wl.Spec.PodSets)
+
+		priorityClassName, source, p, err := r.extractPriority(ctx, wl.Spec.PodSets, job)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		wl.Spec.PriorityClassName = priorityClassName
+		wl.Spec.Priority = &p
+		wl.Spec.PriorityClassSource = source
+
+		return wl, nil
```

  Please address

- **pkg/controller/jobs/pod/pod_controller.go:544** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-11-16T15:34:30Z
```diff
@@ -229,6 +255,266 @@ func (p *Pod) Skip() bool {
 	return false
 }
 
+func (p *Pod) groupName() string {
+	return p.Object().GetLabels()[GroupNameLabel]
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) groupTotalCount() (int, error) {
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("pod doesn't have a '%s' label", GroupNameLabel)
+	}
+
+	gtcAnnotation, ok := p.Object().GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation]
+	if !ok {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	gtc, err := strconv.Atoi(gtcAnnotation)
+	if err != nil {
+		return 0, err
+	}
+
+	if gtc < 1 {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("incorrect annotation value '%s=%s': group total count should be greater than zero",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation, gtcAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	return gtc, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup corev1.PodList) ([]kueue.PodSet, error) {
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+
+	var (
+		resultPodSets []kueue.PodSet
+	)
+
+	for _, podInGroup := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		tc, err := strconv.Atoi(podInGroup.GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation])
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation from the pod '%s': %w",
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				podInGroup.GetName(),
+				err)
+		}
+		if tc != groupTotalCount {
+			// ToDo: Add a warning event
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("pods '%s' and '%s' has different '%s' values: %d!=%d",
+				p.GetName(), podInGroup.GetName(),
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				groupTotalCount, tc)
+		}
+
+		roleHash, ok := podInGroup.Annotations[RoleHashAnnotation]
+		if !ok {
+			roleHash, err = getRoleHash(fromObject(&podInGroup))
+		}
+
+		roleHash = roleHash[:8]
+
+		podRoleFound := false
+		for psi := range resultPodSets {
+			if resultPodSets[psi].Name == roleHash {
+				podRoleFound = true
+				resultPodSets[psi].Count++
+			}
+		}
+
+		if !podRoleFound {
+			podSet := fromObject(&podInGroup).PodSets()
+			podSet[0].Name = roleHash
+
+			resultPodSets = append(resultPodSets, podSet[0])
+		}
+	}
+
+	return resultPodSets, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) ConstructComposableWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets     []kueue.PodSet
+		podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	)
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: p.groupName(),
+		}); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podsInGroup.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+		}
+
+		podSets, err = p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	wl := &kueue.Workload{
+		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+			Namespace:  p.GetNamespace(),
+			Labels:     map[string]string{},
+			Finalizers: []string{kueue.ResourceInUseFinalizerName},
+		},
+		Spec: kueue.WorkloadSpec{
+			PodSets:   podSets,
+			QueueName: jobframework.QueueName(p),
+		},
+	}
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		wl.Name = jobframework.GetWorkloadNameForOwnerWithGVK(p.GetName(), p.GVK())
+		jobUid := string(p.Object().GetUID())
+		if errs := validation.IsValidLabelValue(jobUid); len(errs) == 0 {
+			wl.Labels[controllerconsts.JobUIDLabel] = jobUid
+		} else {
+			log.V(2).Info(
+				"Validation of the owner job UID label has failed. Creating workload without the label.",
+				"ValidationErrors", errs,
+				"LabelValue", jobUid,
+			)
+		}
+
+		// add the owner ref
+		if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(p.Object(), wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	} else {
+		wl.Name = p.groupName()
+		for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+			if err := controllerutil.SetOwnerReference(&pod, wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
```

  Let's put one scenario:
  - The group is of size 1.
  - A pod is preempted for whatever reason, so it has a deletion timestamp.
  - Does the Workload get deleted or get a deletion timestamp at this point?
  
  We don't want that to happen, so a replacement pod for the failed pod can be sent by the user, re-utilizing the same admission.

```diff
+		return nil, err

+		}

+			// ToDo: Add a warning event

+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				groupTotalCount, tc))
+		}
+
+		roleHash, ok := podInGroup.Annotations[RoleHashAnnotation]
+		if !ok {
+			roleHash, err = getRoleHash(fromObject(&podInGroup))
+		}
+
+		podRoleFound := false
+		for psi := range resultPodSets {
+			if resultPodSets[psi].Name == roleHash {
+				podRoleFound = true
+				resultPodSets[psi].Count++
+			}
+		}
+
+		if !podRoleFound {
+			podSet := fromObject(&podInGroup).PodSets()
+			podSet[0].Name = roleHash
+
+			resultPodSets = append(resultPodSets, podSet[0])
+		}
+	}
+
+	slices.SortFunc(resultPodSets, func(a, b kueue.PodSet) int {
+		return cmp.Compare(a.Name, b.Name)
+	})
+
+	return resultPodSets, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) ConstructComposableWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets     []kueue.PodSet
+		podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	)
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: p.groupName(),
+		}); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podsInGroup.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, jobframework.UnretryableError(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+		}
+
+		podSets, err = p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+		if len(podSets) > 8 {
+			return nil, jobframework.UnretryableError(errMsgIncorrectGroupRoleCount)
+		}
+
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	wl := &kueue.Workload{
+		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+			Namespace:  p.GetNamespace(),
+			Labels:     map[string]string{},
+			Finalizers: []string{kueue.ResourceInUseFinalizerName},
+		},
+		Spec: kueue.WorkloadSpec{
+			PodSets:   podSets,
+			QueueName: jobframework.QueueName(p),
+		},
+	}
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		wl.Name = jobframework.GetWorkloadNameForOwnerWithGVK(p.GetName(), p.GVK())
+		jobUid := string(p.Object().GetUID())
+		if errs := validation.IsValidLabelValue(jobUid); len(errs) == 0 {
+			wl.Labels[controllerconsts.JobUIDLabel] = jobUid
+		} else {
+			log.V(2).Info(
+				"Validation of the owner job UID label has failed. Creating workload without the label.",
+				"ValidationErrors", errs,
+				"LabelValue", jobUid,
+			)
+		}
+
+		// add the owner ref
+		if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(p.Object(), wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	} else {
+		wl.Name = p.groupName()
+		for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+			if err := controllerutil.SetOwnerReference(&pod, wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+				return nil, err
+			}
+		}
+	}
+
+	return wl, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx context.Context, c client.Client) (*kueue.Workload, []*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	groupName := p.groupName()
+
+	if groupName == "" {
+		return jobframework.FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx, c, p)
+	}
+
+	// Find a matching workload first if there is one.
+	workload := &kueue.Workload{}
+	if err := c.Get(ctx, types.NamespacedName{Name: p.groupName(), Namespace: p.GetNamespace()}, workload); err != nil {
+		if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+			return nil, nil, nil
+		}
+		log.Error(err, "Unable to get related workload")
+		return nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	var podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+		GroupNameLabel: p.groupName(),
+	}); err != nil {
+		return nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	jobPodSets, err := p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	if p.equivalentToWorkload(workload, jobPodSets) {
+		return workload, []*kueue.Workload{}, nil
+	} else {
+		return nil, []*kueue.Workload{workload}, nil
+	}
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) equivalentToWorkload(wl *kueue.Workload, jobPodSets []kueue.PodSet) bool {
+	workloadFinished := apimeta.FindStatusCondition(wl.Status.Conditions, kueue.WorkloadFinished) != nil
+
+	if wl.GetName() != p.groupName() {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	if !workloadFinished && len(jobPodSets) != len(wl.Spec.PodSets) {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	for i := range wl.Spec.PodSets {
+		if !workloadFinished && wl.Spec.PodSets[i].Count != jobPodSets[i].Count {
+			return false
+		}
+		if i < len(jobPodSets) && wl.Spec.PodSets[i].Name != jobPodSets[i].Name {
+			return false
+		}
+	}
+
+	return true
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) IsComposableJobFinished(ctx context.Context, c client.Client) (metav1.Condition, bool) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	groupName := p.groupName()
+	if groupName == "" {
+		return p.Finished()
+	}
+
+	var podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+		GroupNameLabel: groupName,
+	}); err != nil {
+		return metav1.Condition{}, false
+	}
+
+	succeededPodCount := 0
+
+	for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		if pod.Status.Phase == corev1.PodSucceeded {
+			succeededPodCount++
+		}
+
+		podJob := fromObject(&pod)
+		if _, finished := podJob.Finished(); !finished {
+			return metav1.Condition{}, false
+		}
+	}
+
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		log.V(2).Error(err, "Error while checking if pod group is finished", "Pod.Name", p.Name)
+		return metav1.Condition{}, false
+	}
+
+	condition := metav1.Condition{
+		Type:   kueue.WorkloadFinished,
+		Status: metav1.ConditionTrue,
+		Reason: "JobFinished",
+		Message: fmt.Sprintf(
+			"Pod group has finished. Pods succeeded: %d/%d. Pods failed: %d/%d",
```

  ```suggestion
  			"Pods succeeded: %d/%d. Pods failed: %d/%d",
  ```

```diff
+		if err != nil {

+		}
+	}
+
+	wl := &kueue.Workload{
+		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+			Namespace:  p.GetNamespace(),
+			Labels:     map[string]string{},
+			Finalizers: []string{kueue.ResourceInUseFinalizerName},
+		},
+		Spec: kueue.WorkloadSpec{
+			PodSets:   podSets,
+			QueueName: jobframework.QueueName(p),
+		},
+	}
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		wl.Name = jobframework.GetWorkloadNameForOwnerWithGVK(p.GetName(), p.GVK())
+		jobUid := string(p.Object().GetUID())
+		if errs := validation.IsValidLabelValue(jobUid); len(errs) == 0 {
+			wl.Labels[controllerconsts.JobUIDLabel] = jobUid
+		} else {
+			log.V(2).Info(
+				"Validation of the owner job UID label has failed. Creating workload without the label.",
+				"ValidationErrors", errs,
+				"LabelValue", jobUid,
+			)
+		}
+
+		// add the owner ref
+		if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(p.Object(), wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	} else {
+		wl.Name = p.groupName()
+		for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+			if err := controllerutil.SetOwnerReference(&pod, wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
```

  The older pod will be present in the cluster because of the finalizer. So the workload will not be deleted. The only problem for this scenario is the finalizer removal for the older pod after it has been replaced.

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-11-16T19:40:02Z

- **pkg/controller/jobs/pod/pod_controller.go:544** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-11-16T19:40:02Z
```diff
@@ -229,6 +255,266 @@ func (p *Pod) Skip() bool {
 	return false
 }
 
+func (p *Pod) groupName() string {
+	return p.Object().GetLabels()[GroupNameLabel]
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) groupTotalCount() (int, error) {
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("pod doesn't have a '%s' label", GroupNameLabel)
+	}
+
+	gtcAnnotation, ok := p.Object().GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation]
+	if !ok {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	gtc, err := strconv.Atoi(gtcAnnotation)
+	if err != nil {
+		return 0, err
+	}
+
+	if gtc < 1 {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("incorrect annotation value '%s=%s': group total count should be greater than zero",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation, gtcAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	return gtc, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup corev1.PodList) ([]kueue.PodSet, error) {
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+
+	var (
+		resultPodSets []kueue.PodSet
+	)
+
+	for _, podInGroup := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		tc, err := strconv.Atoi(podInGroup.GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation])
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation from the pod '%s': %w",
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				podInGroup.GetName(),
+				err)
+		}
+		if tc != groupTotalCount {
+			// ToDo: Add a warning event
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("pods '%s' and '%s' has different '%s' values: %d!=%d",
+				p.GetName(), podInGroup.GetName(),
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				groupTotalCount, tc)
+		}
+
+		roleHash, ok := podInGroup.Annotations[RoleHashAnnotation]
+		if !ok {
+			roleHash, err = getRoleHash(fromObject(&podInGroup))
+		}
+
+		roleHash = roleHash[:8]
+
+		podRoleFound := false
+		for psi := range resultPodSets {
+			if resultPodSets[psi].Name == roleHash {
+				podRoleFound = true
+				resultPodSets[psi].Count++
+			}
+		}
+
+		if !podRoleFound {
+			podSet := fromObject(&podInGroup).PodSets()
+			podSet[0].Name = roleHash
+
+			resultPodSets = append(resultPodSets, podSet[0])
+		}
+	}
+
+	return resultPodSets, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) ConstructComposableWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets     []kueue.PodSet
+		podsInGroup corev1.PodList
+	)
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: p.groupName(),
+		}); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podsInGroup.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+		}
+
+		podSets, err = p.constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	}
+
+	wl := &kueue.Workload{
+		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+			Namespace:  p.GetNamespace(),
+			Labels:     map[string]string{},
+			Finalizers: []string{kueue.ResourceInUseFinalizerName},
+		},
+		Spec: kueue.WorkloadSpec{
+			PodSets:   podSets,
+			QueueName: jobframework.QueueName(p),
+		},
+	}
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		wl.Name = jobframework.GetWorkloadNameForOwnerWithGVK(p.GetName(), p.GVK())
+		jobUid := string(p.Object().GetUID())
+		if errs := validation.IsValidLabelValue(jobUid); len(errs) == 0 {
+			wl.Labels[controllerconsts.JobUIDLabel] = jobUid
+		} else {
+			log.V(2).Info(
+				"Validation of the owner job UID label has failed. Creating workload without the label.",
+				"ValidationErrors", errs,
+				"LabelValue", jobUid,
+			)
+		}
+
+		// add the owner ref
+		if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(p.Object(), wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	} else {
+		wl.Name = p.groupName()
+		for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+			if err := controllerutil.SetOwnerReference(&pod, wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
```

  We should only remove all the finalizers at the end, when the Workload is declared finished.

```diff
+// ComposableJob interface should be implemented by generic jobs that
```

```diff
+					AssignmentPodCount(createdWorkload.Spec.PodSets[0].Count).

+				)
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) []corev1.PodSchedulingGate {
```

- **pkg/controller/jobs/pod/pod_controller.go:119** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-11-22T16:37:13Z
```diff
@@ -71,24 +82,71 @@ var NewReconciler = jobframework.NewGenericReconciler(
 		return &Pod{}
 	}, nil)
 
-type Pod corev1.Pod
+type Pod struct {
+	pod     corev1.Pod
+	isGroup bool
+	list    corev1.PodList
+	isFull  bool // if it's fully read
+}
 
-var _ jobframework.GenericJob = (*Pod)(nil)
-var _ jobframework.JobWithCustomStop = (*Pod)(nil)
-var _ jobframework.JobWithFinalize = (*Pod)(nil)
+// Get implements jobframework.ComposableJob.
+func (p *Pod) Get(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, key types.NamespacedName) (err error, removeWlFinalizer bool) {
+	if err := c.Get(ctx, key, &p.pod); err != nil {
+		return err, apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	}
+	groupName := p.groupName()
+	p.isGroup = groupName != ""
+	if !p.isGroup {
+		return nil, !p.pod.DeletionTimestamp.IsZero()
+	}
+
+	if err := c.List(ctx, &p.list, client.MatchingLabels{
+		GroupNameLabel: groupName,
+	}, client.InNamespace(key.Namespace)); err != nil {
+		return err, false
+	}
+
+	p.isFull = true
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		return err, false
+	}
+
+	if len(p.list.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+		return jobframework.UnretryableError(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount), false
+	}
+
+	// remove wl finalizers if all the pods have a deletion timestamp
```

  This is not accurate, as all Pods will have a deletion timestamp when the group is preempted.
  
  In the case of pod group, we require the user action to either explicitly delete the Workload object, or create a Pod with the `retriable-in-group: false` annotation. We will only remove the Workload finalizer when we are sure that the workload is finished.
  
  For the purpose of this PR, we can do the happy path.

- **pkg/controller/jobs/pod/pod_controller.go:109** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-11-22T16:42:37Z
```diff
@@ -71,24 +82,71 @@ var NewReconciler = jobframework.NewGenericReconciler(
 		return &Pod{}
 	}, nil)
 
-type Pod corev1.Pod
+type Pod struct {
+	pod     corev1.Pod
+	isGroup bool
+	list    corev1.PodList
+	isFull  bool // if it's fully read
+}
 
-var _ jobframework.GenericJob = (*Pod)(nil)
-var _ jobframework.JobWithCustomStop = (*Pod)(nil)
-var _ jobframework.JobWithFinalize = (*Pod)(nil)
+// Get implements jobframework.ComposableJob.
+func (p *Pod) Get(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, key types.NamespacedName) (err error, removeWlFinalizer bool) {
+	if err := c.Get(ctx, key, &p.pod); err != nil {
+		return err, apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	}
+	groupName := p.groupName()
+	p.isGroup = groupName != ""
+	if !p.isGroup {
+		return nil, !p.pod.DeletionTimestamp.IsZero()
+	}
+
+	if err := c.List(ctx, &p.list, client.MatchingLabels{
+		GroupNameLabel: groupName,
+	}, client.InNamespace(key.Namespace)); err != nil {
+		return err, false
+	}
+
+	p.isFull = true
```

  I don't think this is the right time to check if the group is full.
  
  We want to make sure the group is full before we create the first Workload object. But once the Workload object is created, we should still reconcile the group, as the user might be in the process of creating replacement Pods or maybe it will decide to delete the Workload object.

```diff
+// PodsReady instructs whether job derived pods are all ready now.
+func (p *Pod) PodsReady() bool {
+	if !p.isGroup {
+		return hasPodReadyTrue(p.pod.Status.Conditions)
+	}
+
+	for i := range p.list.Items {
+		if !hasPodReadyTrue(p.list.Items[i].Status.Conditions) {
+			return false
+		}
+	}
+	return true

+func (p *Pod) groupName() string {
+	return p.Object().GetLabels()[GroupNameLabel]
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) groupTotalCount() (int, error) {
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("pod doesn't have a '%s' label", GroupNameLabel)
+	}
+
+	gtcAnnotation, ok := p.Object().GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation]
+	if !ok {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	gtc, err := strconv.Atoi(gtcAnnotation)
+	if err != nil {
+		return 0, err
+	}
+
+	if gtc < 1 {
+		return 0, fmt.Errorf("incorrect annotation value '%s=%s': group total count should be greater than zero",
+			GroupTotalCountAnnotation, gtcAnnotation)
+	}
+
+	return gtc, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) constructGroupPodSets(podsInGroup corev1.PodList) ([]kueue.PodSet, error) {
+	groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+	originalQueue := jobframework.QueueName(p)
+
+	var resultPodSets []kueue.PodSet
+
+	for _, podInGroup := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		// Skip failed pods
+		if podInGroup.Status.Phase == corev1.PodFailed {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if podInGroupQueue := jobframework.QueueNameForObject(&podInGroup); podInGroupQueue != originalQueue {
+			return nil, jobframework.UnretryableError(fmt.Sprintf("pods '%s' and '%s' has different queue names: %s!=%s",
+				p.pod.GetName(), podInGroup.GetName(),
+				originalQueue, podInGroupQueue))
+		}
+
+		tc, err := strconv.Atoi(podInGroup.GetAnnotations()[GroupTotalCountAnnotation])
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to extract '%s' annotation from the pod '%s': %w",
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				podInGroup.GetName(),
+				err)
+		}
+		if tc != groupTotalCount {
+			return nil, jobframework.UnretryableError(fmt.Sprintf("pods '%s' and '%s' has different '%s' values: %d!=%d",
+				p.pod.GetName(), podInGroup.GetName(),
+				GroupTotalCountAnnotation,
+				groupTotalCount, tc))
+		}
+
+		roleHash, ok := podInGroup.Annotations[RoleHashAnnotation]
+		if !ok {
+			roleHash, err = getRoleHash(fromObject(&podInGroup))
+			if err != nil {
+				return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to calculate role hash for the pod with no '%s' annotation. %w", RoleHashAnnotation, err)
+			}
+		}
+
+		podRoleFound := false
+		for psi := range resultPodSets {
+			if resultPodSets[psi].Name == roleHash {
+				podRoleFound = true
+				resultPodSets[psi].Count++
+			}
+		}
+
+		if !podRoleFound {
+			podSet := fromObject(&podInGroup).PodSets()
+			podSet[0].Name = roleHash
+
+			resultPodSets = append(resultPodSets, podSet[0])
+		}
+	}
+
+	slices.SortFunc(resultPodSets, func(a, b kueue.PodSet) int {
+		return cmp.Compare(a.Name, b.Name)
+	})
+
+	return resultPodSets, nil
+}
+

+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets []kueue.PodSet
+	)
+
+	if !p.isGroup {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		//TODO: do someting if not filly read
```

```diff
+func (p *Pod) ConstructComposableWorkload(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, r record.EventRecorder) (*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	object := p.Object()
+
+	var (
+		podSets []kueue.PodSet
+	)
+
+	if !p.isGroup {
+		podSets = p.PodSets()
+	} else {
+		//TODO: do someting if not filly read
+		groupTotalCount, err := p.groupTotalCount()
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(p.list.Items) != groupTotalCount {
+			r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+			return nil, jobframework.UnretryableError(errMsgIncorrectTotalGroupCount)
+		}
+
+		podSets, err = p.constructGroupPodSets(p.list)
+		if err != nil {
+			if jobframework.IsUnretryableError(err) {
+				r.Eventf(object, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "ErrWorkloadCompose", err.Error())
+			}
+			return nil, err
+		}
+
+		if len(podSets) > 8 {
+			return nil, jobframework.UnretryableError(errMsgIncorrectGroupRoleCount)
+		}
+	}
+
+	wl := &kueue.Workload{
+		ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+			Namespace:  p.pod.GetNamespace(),
+			Labels:     map[string]string{},
+			Finalizers: []string{kueue.ResourceInUseFinalizerName},
+		},
+		Spec: kueue.WorkloadSpec{
+			PodSets:   podSets,
+			QueueName: jobframework.QueueName(p),
+		},
+	}
+
+	if p.groupName() == "" {
+		wl.Name = jobframework.GetWorkloadNameForOwnerWithGVK(p.pod.GetName(), p.GVK())
+		jobUid := string(p.Object().GetUID())
+		if errs := validation.IsValidLabelValue(jobUid); len(errs) == 0 {
+			wl.Labels[controllerconsts.JobUIDLabel] = jobUid
+		} else {
+			log.V(2).Info(
+				"Validation of the owner job UID label has failed. Creating workload without the label.",
+				"ValidationErrors", errs,
+				"LabelValue", jobUid,
+			)
+		}
+
+		// add the owner ref
+		if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(p.Object(), wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+	} else {
+		wl.Name = p.groupName()
+		for _, pod := range p.list.Items {
+			if err := controllerutil.SetOwnerReference(&pod, wl, c.Scheme()); err != nil {
+				return nil, err
+			}
+		}
+	}
+
+	return wl, nil
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx context.Context, c client.Client) (*kueue.Workload, []*kueue.Workload, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	groupName := p.groupName()
+
+	if groupName == "" {
+		return jobframework.FindMatchingWorkloads(ctx, c, p)
+	}
+
+	// Find a matching workload first if there is one.
+	workload := &kueue.Workload{}
+	if err := c.Get(ctx, types.NamespacedName{Name: p.groupName(), Namespace: p.pod.GetNamespace()}, workload); err != nil {
+		if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+			return nil, nil, nil
+		}
+		log.Error(err, "Unable to get related workload")
+		return nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	jobPodSets, err := p.constructGroupPodSets(p.list)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, nil, err
+	}
+
+	if p.equivalentToWorkload(workload, jobPodSets) {
+		return workload, []*kueue.Workload{}, nil
+	} else {
+		return nil, []*kueue.Workload{workload}, nil
+	}
+}
+
+func (p *Pod) equivalentToWorkload(wl *kueue.Workload, jobPodSets []kueue.PodSet) bool {
+	workloadFinished := apimeta.IsStatusConditionTrue(wl.Status.Conditions, kueue.WorkloadFinished)
+
+	if wl.GetName() != p.groupName() {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	if !workloadFinished && len(wl.Spec.PodSets) < len(jobPodSets) {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	for i := range wl.Spec.PodSets {
+		if i >= len(jobPodSets) {
+			return true
+		}
+		if !workloadFinished && wl.Spec.PodSets[i].Count < jobPodSets[i].Count {
+			return false
+		}
+		if wl.Spec.PodSets[i].Name != jobPodSets[i].Name {
+			return false
+		}
```

  Let's imagine there are 2 podsets, each with 1 pod.
  
  If one of the pods is missing, the equivalency check should pass. I don't this code is letting that pass.

  Let's add these cases:
  - a Pod group of 1, there is a Failed Pod and a Pod with a scheduling gate. The scheduling gate should be removed.
  - a Pod group of 2, and there are 2 Succeeded Pods and one Failed Pod. The workload should be considered Finished.
  - a Pod group of 1, the Pod has a deletionTimestamp, but phase Running. The workload initially has an Evicted condition, but still has the QuotaReservation. The workload should remain the same.
  - a Pod group of 1, the Pod has a deletionTimestamp, but phase Failed. The workload initially has an Evicted condition, but still has the QuotaReservation. The workload should get the reservation cleared.

- **pkg/controller/jobs/pod/pod_webhook.go:141** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-11-22T18:04:30Z
```diff
@@ -77,9 +87,89 @@ func SetupWebhook(mgr ctrl.Manager, opts ...jobframework.Option) error {
 
 var _ webhook.CustomDefaulter = &PodWebhook{}
 
+func omitKueueLabels(l map[string]string) map[string]string {
+	result := map[string]string{}
+
+	for key, value := range l {
+		if !strings.HasPrefix(key, "kueue.x-k8s.io/") {
+			result[key] = value
+		}
+	}
+	return result
+}
+
+func containersShape(containers []corev1.Container) (result []map[string]interface{}) {
+	for _, c := range containers {
+		result = append(result, map[string]interface{}{
+			"image": c.Image,
+			"resources": map[string]interface{}{
+				"requests": c.Resources.Requests,
+			},
+			"ports": c.Ports,
+		})
+	}
+
+	return result
+}
+
+func volumesShape(volumes []corev1.Volume) (result []corev1.Volume) {
+	for _, v := range volumes {
+		v.Name = ""
+		result = append(result, v)
+	}
+
+	return result
+}
+
+func getRoleHash(p *Pod) (string, error) {
+
+	shape := map[string]interface{}{
+		"metadata": map[string]interface{}{
+			"labels": omitKueueLabels(p.pod.ObjectMeta.Labels),
+		},
+		"spec": map[string]interface{}{
+			"initContainers":            containersShape(p.pod.Spec.InitContainers),
+			"containers":                containersShape(p.pod.Spec.Containers),
+			"nodeSelector":              p.pod.Spec.NodeSelector,
+			"affinity":                  p.pod.Spec.Affinity,
+			"tolerations":               p.pod.Spec.Tolerations,
+			"runtimeClassName":          p.pod.Spec.RuntimeClassName,
+			"priority":                  p.pod.Spec.Priority,
+			"preemptionPolicy":          p.pod.Spec.PreemptionPolicy,
+			"topologySpreadConstraints": p.pod.Spec.TopologySpreadConstraints,
+			"overhead":                  p.pod.Spec.Overhead,
+			"volumes":                   volumesShape(p.pod.Spec.Volumes),
```

  oh cool. We might need to do the same for resourceClaims, but let's leave that for a follow up.

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-11-22T18:11:39Z

```diff
@@ -128,11 +134,69 @@ func DeleteAllJobsInNamespace(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, ns *corev1.N
 	return nil
 }
 
+func DeleteAllPodsInNamespace(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, ns *corev1.Namespace) error {
+	err := c.DeleteAllOf(ctx, &corev1.Pod{}, client.InNamespace(ns.Name))
+	if err != nil && !apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+		return err
+	}
+
+	lst := corev1.PodList{}
+	err = c.List(ctx, &lst, client.InNamespace(ns.Name))
+	if err != nil && !apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+		return err
+	}
+
+	if len(lst.Items) == 0 {
+		return nil
+	}
+
+	for _, p := range lst.Items {
+		copy := p.DeepCopy()
+		if controllerutil.RemoveFinalizer(copy, pod.PodFinalizer) {
+			err = c.Update(ctx, copy)
+			if err != nil && !apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+				return err
+			}
+		}
+	}
+
+	return nil
+}
+
 func DeleteWorkloadsInNamespace(ctx context.Context, c client.Client, ns *corev1.Namespace) error {
 	if err := c.DeleteAllOf(ctx, &kueue.Workload{}, client.InNamespace(ns.Name)); err != nil && !apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
 		return err
 	}
-	return nil
+
+	err := wait.ExponentialBackoffWithContext(ctx,
```

  Since we are already using `gomega` in this package, prefer to use `Eventually` here.
  
  Why don't we need the same retry logic for deleting Pods?

```diff
+					Obj(),

+					Clone().
+					Name("pod2").
+					Label("kueue.x-k8s.io/managed", "true").

+					Group("test-group").
+					GroupTotalCount("2").
+					StatusPhase(corev1.PodSucceeded).
+					Obj(),

+
```

```diff
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, pod2)).Should(gomega.Succeed())

+				return k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlLookupKey, createdWorkload)

+

+			gomega.Expect(createdWorkload.Spec.PodSets[0].Count).To(gomega.Equal(int32(2)))
+			gomega.Expect(createdWorkload.Spec.PodSets[0].Name).To(gomega.Equal("120fa2c0"))
```

```diff
+			createdPod2 := &corev1.Pod{}

+					AssignmentPodCount(createdWorkload.Spec.PodSets[0].Count).
+					Obj()

+
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) []corev1.PodSchedulingGate {

+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, pod2LookupKey, createdPod2)).To(gomega.Succeed())

+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).ShouldNot(
+					gomega.ContainElement(corev1.PodSchedulingGate{Name: "kueue.x-k8s.io/admission"}),
```

  I think the implementation as it is should be ready to support  one more case:
  
  1. Create pod group of size 1
  2. Admit workload
  3. fail the pod
  4. create a new pod in the same group
  5. mark the new pod as succeeded
  6. verify workload is marked as finished

  We can add more steps to this test:
  
  1. The workload is readmitted
  2. There are new pods in the group
  3. The pods succeed.
  
  Then this would be a full test for preemption and recovery.

```diff
+		c := conds[i]
 		if c.Type == corev1.PodReady {
 			return c.Status == corev1.ConditionTrue
 		}
 	}
 	return false
 }
 
+// PodsReady instructs whether job derived pods are all ready now.
+func (p *Pod) PodsReady() bool {
+	if !p.isGroup {
+		return hasPodReadyTrue(p.pod.Status.Conditions)
+	}
+
+	for i := range p.list.Items {
+		if !hasPodReadyTrue(p.list.Items[i].Status.Conditions) {
+			return false
+		}
+	}
+	return true
+}
+
 // GVK returns GVK (Group Version Kind) for the job.
 func (p *Pod) GVK() schema.GroupVersionKind {
 	return gvk
 }

 func SetupIndexes(ctx context.Context, indexer client.FieldIndexer) error {

 func (p *Pod) Finalize(ctx context.Context, c client.Client) error {
-	if controllerutil.RemoveFinalizer(p.Object(), PodFinalizer) {

+		podsInGroup.Items = append(podsInGroup.Items, *p.Object().(*corev1.Pod))
+	} else {
+		if err := c.List(ctx, &podsInGroup, client.MatchingLabels{
+			GroupNameLabel: groupName,
+		}, client.InNamespace(p.pod.Namespace)); err != nil {
 			return err
 		}
 	}
 
+	for _, pod := range podsInGroup.Items {
+		if controllerutil.RemoveFinalizer(&pod, PodFinalizer) {
+			if err := c.Update(ctx, &pod); err != nil {
+				return err
+			}
+		}
+	}
+
 	return nil
 }
 
 func (p *Pod) Skip() bool {
 	// Skip pod reconciliation, if managed label is not set
-	if v, ok := p.GetLabels()[ManagedLabelKey]; !ok || v != ManagedLabelValue {

 		return true
 	}
```
